package org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.string;

import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.decode.SourceData;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.Context;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.FunctionConstant;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.TransformFunction;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.operator.OperatorTools;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.parser.ValueParser;

import net.sf.jsqlparser.expression.Function;

import java.net.URLDecoder;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;

/**
 * UrlDecodeFunction  ->  url_decode(str)
 * description:
 * - Return NULL if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an illegal
 *          escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;
 * - Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the UTF-8 encoding scheme.
 */
@TransformFunction(type = FunctionConstant.STRING_TYPE, names = {
        "url_decode"}, parameter = "(String str)", descriptions = {
                "- Return \"\" if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an "
                        +
                        "illegal escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;",
                "- Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the "
                        +
                        "UTF-8 encoding scheme."
        }, examples = {
                "url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fapache.inlong.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode') = \"https://apache.inlong.com/search?q=java url encode\""})
public class UrlDecodeFunction implements ValueParser {

    private final ValueParser stringParser;

    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expr.getParameters().getExpressions().get(0));
    }

    @Override
    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
        if (stringObj == null) {
            return null;
        }
        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
        if (string == null) {
            return null;
        }

        try {
            return URLDecoder.decode(string, StandardCharsets.UTF_8.toString());
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
}

package org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.string;

import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.decode.SourceDecoderFactory;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.encode.SinkEncoderFactory;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.pojo.TransformConfig;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.TransformProcessor;

import org.junit.Assert;
import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;

public class TestUrlDecodeFunction extends AbstractFunctionStringTestBase {

    @Test
    public void testUrlDecodeFunction() throws Exception {
        String transformSql = "select url_decode(string1) from source";
        TransformConfig config = new TransformConfig(transformSql);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor = TransformProcessor
                .create(config, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));

        // case1: url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode')
        List<String> output1 = processor.transform(
                "https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
        Assert.assertEquals(1, output1.size());
        Assert.assertEquals(output1.get(0), "result=https://www.google.com/search?q=java url encode");

        String transformSql2 = "select url_decode(stringX) from source";
        TransformConfig config2 = new TransformConfig(transformSql2);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor2 = TransformProcessor
                .create(config2, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));
        // case2: url_decode(null)
        List<String> output2 = processor2.transform("|apple|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
        Assert.assertEquals(1, output2.size());
        Assert.assertEquals(output2.get(0), "result=");
    }
}

    public void testUrlDecodeFunction() throws Exception {
        String transformSql = "select url_decode(string1) from source";
        TransformConfig config = new TransformConfig(transformSql);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor = TransformProcessor
                .create(config, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));

        // case1: url_decode('"'"'https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode'"'"')
        List<String> output1 = processor.transform(
                "https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
        Assert.assertEquals(1, output1.size());
        Assert.assertEquals(output1.get(0), "result=https://www.google.com/search?q=java url encode");

        String transformSql2 = "select url_decode(stringX) from source";
        TransformConfig config2 = new TransformConfig(transformSql2);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor2 = TransformProcessor

package org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.string;

import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.decode.SourceDecoderFactory;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.encode.SinkEncoderFactory;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.pojo.TransformConfig;
import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.TransformProcessor;

import org.junit.Assert;
import org.junit.Test;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;

public class TestUrlDecodeFunction extends AbstractFunctionStringTestBase {

    @Test
    public void testUrlDecodeFunction() throws Exception {
        String transformSql = "select url_decode(string1) from source";
        TransformConfig config = new TransformConfig(transformSql);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor = TransformProcessor
                .create(config, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));

        // case1: url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode')
        List<String> output1 = processor.transform(
                "https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
        Assert.assertEquals(1, output1.size());
        Assert.assertEquals(output1.get(0), "result=https://www.google.com/search?q=java url encode");

        String transformSql2 = "select url_decode(stringX) from source";
        TransformConfig config2 = new TransformConfig(transformSql2);
        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor2 = TransformProcessor
                .create(config2, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));
        // case2: url_decode(null)
        List<String> output2 = processor2.transform("|apple|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
        Assert.assertEquals(1, output2.size());
        Assert.assertEquals(output2.get(0), "result=");
    }
}

' --new_str '    private final ValueParser stringParser;
    private final ValueParser charsetParser;

    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
        List<Expression> expressions = expr.getParameters().getExpressions();
        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(0));
        if (expressions.size() > 1) {
            charsetParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(1));
        } else {
            charsetParser = null;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
        if (stringObj == null) {
            return null;
        }
        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
        if (string == null) {
            return null;
        }

        String charset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8.toString();
        if (charsetParser != null) {
            Object charsetObj = charsetParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
            if (charsetObj != null) {
                charset = OperatorTools.parseString(charsetObj);
            }
        }

        try {
            return URLDecoder.decode(string, charset);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
'

    25	import org.junit.Assert;

    30	
    31	public class TestUrlDecodeFunction extends AbstractFunctionStringTestBase {
    32	
    33	    @Test
    34	    public void testUrlDecodeFunction() throws Exception {
    35	        String transformSql = "select url_decode(string1) from source";
    36	        TransformConfig config = new TransformConfig(transformSql);
    37	        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor = TransformProcessor
    38	                .create(config, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
    39	                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));
    40	
    41	        // case1: url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode')
    42	        List<String> output1 = processor.transform(
    43	                "https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
    44	        Assert.assertEquals(1, output1.size());
    45	        Assert.assertEquals(output1.get(0), "result=https://www.google.com/search?q=java url encode");
    46	
    47	        String transformSql2 = "select url_decode(stringX) from source";
    48	        TransformConfig config2 = new TransformConfig(transformSql2);
    49	        TransformProcessor<String, String> processor2 = TransformProcessor
    50	                .create(config2, SourceDecoderFactory.createCsvDecoder(csvSource),
    51	                        SinkEncoderFactory.createKvEncoder(kvSink));
    52	        // case2: url_decode(null)
    53	        List<String> output2 = processor2.transform("|apple|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());
    54	        Assert.assertEquals(1, output2.size());
    55	        Assert.assertEquals(output2.get(0), "result=");
    56	    }
    57	}

    18	package org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.string;
    19	
    20	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.decode.SourceData;
    21	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.Context;
    22	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.FunctionConstant;
    23	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.TransformFunction;
    24	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.operator.OperatorTools;
    25	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.parser.ValueParser;
    26	
    27	import net.sf.jsqlparser.expression.Function;
    28	
    29	import java.net.URLDecoder;
    30	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * UrlDecodeFunction  ->  url_decode(str)
    34	 * description:
    35	 * - Return NULL if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an illegal
    36	 *          escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;
    37	 * - Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the UTF-8 encoding scheme.
    38	 */
    39	@TransformFunction(type = FunctionConstant.STRING_TYPE, names = {
    40	        "url_decode"}, parameter = "(String str)", descriptions = {
    41	                "- Return \"\" if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an "
    42	                        +
    43	                        "illegal escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;",
    44	                "- Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the "
    45	                        +
    46	                        "UTF-8 encoding scheme."
    47	        }, examples = {
    48	                "url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fapache.inlong.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode') = \"https://apache.inlong.com/search?q=java url encode\""})
    49	public class UrlDecodeFunction implements ValueParser {
    50	
    51	    private final ValueParser stringParser;
    52	
    53	    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
    54	        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expr.getParameters().getExpressions().get(0));
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    @Override
    58	    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
    59	        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
    60	        if (stringObj == null) {
    61	            return null;
    62	        }
    63	        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
    64	        if (string == null) {
    65	            return null;
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        try {
    69	            return URLDecoder.decode(string, StandardCharsets.UTF_8.toString());
    70	        } catch (Exception e) {
    71	            return null;
    72	        }
    73	    }
    74	}

' --new_str '/**
 * UrlDecodeFunction  ->  url_decode(str [, charset])
 * description:
 * - Return NULL if '"'"'str'"'"' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an illegal
 *          escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;
 * - Return the result of decoding a given '"'"'str'"'"' in '"'"'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'"'"' format using the UTF-8 encoding scheme
 *          or specified character sets.
 */
@TransformFunction(type = FunctionConstant.STRING_TYPE, names = {
        "url_decode"}, parameter = "(String str [, String charset])", descriptions = {
                "- Return \"\" if '"'"'str'"'"' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an "
                        +
                        "illegal escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;",
                "- Return the result of decoding a given '"'"'str'"'"' in '"'"'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'"'"' format using the "
                        +
                        "UTF-8 encoding scheme or specified character sets."
        }, examples = {
                "url_decode('"'"'https%3A%2F%2Fapache.inlong.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode'"'"') = \"https://apache.inlong.com/search?q=java url encode\"",
                "url_decode('"'"'%CE%D2%BA%C7'"'"', '"'"'GBK'"'"') = \"你好\""})
public class UrlDecodeFunction implements ValueParser {

    private final ValueParser stringParser;
    private final ValueParser charsetParser;

    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
        List<Expression> expressions = expr.getParameters().getExpressions();
        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(0));
        if (expressions.size() > 1) {
            charsetParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(1));
        } else {
            charsetParser = null;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
        if (stringObj == null) {
            return null;
        }
        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
        if (string == null) {
            return null;
        }

        String charset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8.name();
        if (charsetParser != null) {
            Object charsetObj = charsetParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
            if (charsetObj != null) {
                charset = OperatorTools.parseString(charsetObj);
            }
        }

        try {
            return URLDecoder.decode(string, charset);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
}

    36	        TransformConfig config = new TransformConfig(transformSql);

    43	                "https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());

    46

    53	        List<String> output2 = processor2.transform("|apple|banana|cloud|1", new HashMap<>());

    18	package org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.string;
    19	
    20	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.decode.SourceData;
    21	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.Context;
    22	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.FunctionConstant;
    23	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.function.TransformFunction;
    24	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.operator.OperatorTools;
    25	import org.apache.inlong.sdk.transform.process.parser.ValueParser;
    26	
    27	import net.sf.jsqlparser.expression.Function;
    28	
    29	import java.net.URLDecoder;
    30	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * UrlDecodeFunction  ->  url_decode(str)
    34	 * description:
    35	 * - Return NULL if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an illegal
    36	 *          escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;
    37	 * - Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the UTF-8 encoding scheme.
    38	 */
    39	@TransformFunction(type = FunctionConstant.STRING_TYPE, names = {
    40	        "url_decode"}, parameter = "(String str)", descriptions = {
    41	                "- Return \"\" if 'str' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an "
    42	                        +
    43	                        "illegal escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;",
    44	                "- Return the result of decoding a given 'str' in 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' format using the "
    45	                        +
    46	                        "UTF-8 encoding scheme."
    47	        }, examples = {
    48	                "url_decode('https%3A%2F%2Fapache.inlong.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode') = \"https://apache.inlong.com/search?q=java url encode\""})
    49	public class UrlDecodeFunction implements ValueParser {
    50	
    51	    private final ValueParser stringParser;
    52	
    53	    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
    54	        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expr.getParameters().getExpressions().get(0));
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    @Override
    58	    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
    59	        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
    60	        if (stringObj == null) {
    61	            return null;
    62	        }
    63	        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
    64	        if (string == null) {
    65	            return null;
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        try {
    69	            return URLDecoder.decode(string, StandardCharsets.UTF_8.toString());
    70	        } catch (Exception e) {
    71	            return null;
    72	        }
    73	    }
    74	}

' --new_str '/**
 * UrlDecodeFunction  ->  url_decode(str [, charset])
 * description:
 * - Return NULL if '"'"'str'"'"' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an illegal
 *          escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;
 * - Return the result of decoding a given '"'"'str'"'"' in '"'"'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'"'"' format using the UTF-8 encoding scheme
 *          or specified character sets.
 */
@TransformFunction(type = FunctionConstant.STRING_TYPE, names = {
        "url_decode"}, parameter = "(String str [, String charset])", descriptions = {
                "- Return \"\" if '"'"'str'"'"' is NULL, or there is an issue with the decoding process(such as encountering an "
                        +
                        "illegal escape pattern), or the encoding scheme is not supported;",
                "- Return the result of decoding a given '"'"'str'"'"' in '"'"'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'"'"' format using the "
                        +
                        "UTF-8 encoding scheme or specified character sets."
        }, examples = {
                "url_decode('"'"'https%3A%2F%2Fapache.inlong.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Djava+url+encode'"'"') = \"https://apache.inlong.com/search?q=java url encode\"",
                "url_decode('"'"'%CE%D2%BA%C7'"'"', '"'"'GBK'"'"') = \"你好\""})
public class UrlDecodeFunction implements ValueParser {

    private final ValueParser stringParser;
    private final ValueParser charsetParser;

    public UrlDecodeFunction(Function expr) {
        List<Expression> expressions = expr.getParameters().getExpressions();
        stringParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(0));
        if (expressions.size() > 1) {
            charsetParser = OperatorTools.buildParser(expressions.get(1));
        } else {
            charsetParser = null;
        }
    }

    @Override
    public Object parse(SourceData sourceData, int rowIndex, Context context) {
        Object stringObj = stringParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
        if (stringObj == null) {
            return null;
        }
        String string = OperatorTools.parseString(stringObj);
        if (string == null) {
            return null;
        }

        String charset = StandardCharsets.UTF_8.name();
        if (charsetParser != null) {
            Object charsetObj = charsetParser.parse(sourceData, rowIndex, context);
            if (charsetObj != null) {
                charset = OperatorTools.parseString(charsetObj);
            }
        }

        try {
            return URLDecoder.decode(string, charset);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
}
